{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01ShTTxDyoaUABwty88XeJj9","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_014bQETtWbjL7Zjk9eJgHP4u","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/RELEASE_NOTES.md","content":"# Flipt Release Notes\n\n## Overview\n\nThis release focuses on improving OpenTelemetry tracing instrumentation, enabling more flexible distributed tracing configurations and better observability for Flipt deployments.\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\nNone in this release.\n\n## New Features\n\n### Enhanced OpenTelemetry Tracing Configuration\n\n#### Trace Sampling Ratio (`tracing.samplingRatio`)\n\n**New Configuration Option**\n\n- **Type**: Float (0.0 - 1.0)\n- **Default**: 1.0 (sample all traces)\n- **Description**: Controls the sampling ratio for OpenTelemetry traces, allowing you to reduce trace volume in high-throughput environments\n\n**YAML Configuration Example**:\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  samplingRatio: 0.1  # Sample 10% of traces\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: localhost:4317\n```\n\n**Environment Variable**: `FLIPT_TRACING_SAMPLINGRATIO=0.1`\n\n**Use Cases**:\n- Reduce trace storage costs in production environments\n- Sample traces probabilistically based on deployment needs\n- Balance observability with infrastructure costs\n\n---\n\n#### Trace Context Propagators (`tracing.propagators`)\n\n**New Configuration Option**\n\n- **Type**: Array of strings\n- **Default**: `[\"tracecontext\", \"baggage\"]`\n- **Options**:\n  - `tracecontext` — W3C Trace Context standard\n  - `baggage` — W3C Baggage specification\n  - `b3` — Zipkin B3 single-header format\n  - `b3multi` — Zipkin B3 multi-header format\n  - `jaeger` — Jaeger propagation format\n  - `xray` — AWS X-Ray propagation format\n  - `ottrace` — OpenTracing format\n  - `none` — No propagation\n\n**YAML Configuration Example**:\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  propagators:\n    - tracecontext    # W3C standard\n    - baggage         # For context baggage\n    - b3multi         # For Zipkin compatibility\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: localhost:4317\n```\n\n**Environment Variable**:\n```bash\nFLIPT_TRACING_PROPAGATORS=\"tracecontext,baggage,b3multi\"\n```\n\n**Use Cases**:\n- Multi-vendor tracing environments (mix of OpenTelemetry collectors, Zipkin, Jaeger, AWS X-Ray)\n- Propagate custom baggage context across service boundaries\n- Maintain compatibility with existing distributed tracing infrastructure\n\n---\n\n### Improved OpenTelemetry Resource Attributes\n\nThe tracer provider now initializes with comprehensive resource information:\n\n- **Service Name**: \"flipt\"\n- **Service Version**: Flipt version number\n- **Schema URL**: Latest OpenTelemetry semantic conventions (v1.24.0)\n- **Environment Variables**: OTEL_RESOURCE_ATTRIBUTES support\n- **Telemetry SDK Information**: Automatic SDK version and language attributes\n- **Container Information**: Container ID, image, etc. (when available)\n- **Host Information**: Hostname, OS, architecture\n- **Process Runtime Information**: Runtime name, version, and description\n\n**Impact**: Better observability with richer trace context for correlation and debugging\n\n---\n\n### Feature Flags Semantic Conventions\n\nFlipt now uses OpenTelemetry semantic conventions for feature flag operations in traces:\n\n- **`flipt.flag`**: Flag key being evaluated\n- **`flipt.namespace`**: Namespace key for the flag\n- **`flipt.flag_enabled`**: Whether the flag is enabled\n- **`flipt.match`**: Whether evaluation matched a rule\n- **`flipt.segment`**: Matched segment (if applicable)\n- **`flipt.segments`**: List of matched segments\n- **`flipt.reason`**: Evaluation reason (e.g., FLAG_DISABLED, MATCH, NOT_FOUND)\n- **`flipt.value`**: Flag value returned\n- **`flipt.entity_id`**: Entity ID used for evaluation\n- **`flipt.request_id`**: Request correlation ID\n\nPlus standard OpenTelemetry feature flag attributes:\n- **`feature_flag.key`**: Feature flag key (W3C standard)\n- **`feature_flag.provider_name`**: Provider name (\"Flipt\")\n- **`feature_flag.variant`**: Returned variant key\n\nSee [OpenTelemetry Feature Flags Semantic Conventions](https://opentelemetry.io/docs/specs/semconv/feature-flags/feature-flags-spans/) for details.\n\n---\n\n## Deprecations\n\n### Jaeger Tracing Exporter\n\n**Status**: Deprecated (since v1.36.0)\n\nThe Jaeger tracing exporter is **not recommended** for new deployments.\n\n**Reason**: OpenTelemetry officially dropped support for the Jaeger exporter in July 2023. Jaeger itself recommends using OTLP (OpenTelemetry Protocol) for new integrations.\n\n**Migration Path**: Use OTLP exporter instead\n\n=== Before (Deprecated)\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: jaeger\n  jaeger:\n    host: localhost\n    port: 6831\n```\n\n=== After (Recommended)\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: localhost:4317\n```\n\nJaeger receivers OTLP natively, so this is a drop-in replacement. Configure your Jaeger deployment to receive OTLP traces:\n\n```yaml\n# jaeger-collector configuration\nreceivers:\n  otlp:\n    protocols:\n      grpc:\n        endpoint: localhost:4317\n```\n\n**Removal Timeline**: Will be removed after ~1 year from v1.36.0 (deprecated approximately 2024)\n\n---\n\n## Configuration Schema Updates\n\nThe JSON schema for Flipt configuration (`config/flipt.schema.json`) has been updated with:\n\n1. **`tracing.samplingRatio`** property\n   - Type: number\n   - Minimum: 0, Maximum: 1\n   - Default: 1\n\n2. **`tracing.propagators`** property\n   - Type: array of strings\n   - Items: enum of propagator types\n   - Default: `[\"tracecontext\", \"baggage\"]`\n\n---\n\n## Upgrade Guide\n\n### For Existing Users\n\n**If you don't use tracing**, no action is required. This release is fully backward compatible.\n\n### To Enable the New Features\n\n#### Step 1: Upgrade Flipt\n\n```bash\n# Using Docker\ndocker pull flipt/flipt:latest\n\n# Or build from source\ngo build -o flipt ./cmd/flipt\n```\n\n#### Step 2: Configure Sampling (Optional)\n\nIf running Flipt in a high-throughput environment and want to reduce trace volume:\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  samplingRatio: 0.1  # Sample 10% of traces\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: localhost:4317\n```\n\nOr via environment variable:\n```bash\nexport FLIPT_TRACING_SAMPLINGRATIO=0.1\n```\n\n#### Step 3: Configure Propagators (Optional)\n\nIf you have a multi-vendor tracing setup:\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  propagators:\n    - tracecontext\n    - baggage\n    - b3multi  # Add Zipkin B3 support\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: localhost:4317\n```\n\nOr via environment variable:\n```bash\nexport FLIPT_TRACING_PROPAGATORS=\"tracecontext,baggage,b3multi\"\n```\n\n#### Step 4: Update Jaeger Deployments (If Applicable)\n\nIf you're currently using the Jaeger exporter, migrate to OTLP:\n\n**Old Configuration**:\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: jaeger\n  jaeger:\n    host: jaeger-collector\n    port: 6831\n```\n\n**New Configuration**:\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: jaeger-collector:4317\n```\n\nEnsure your Jaeger collector is configured to receive OTLP:\n```yaml\nreceivers:\n  otlp:\n    protocols:\n      grpc:\n        endpoint: 0.0.0.0:4317\n```\n\n#### Step 5: Validate Configuration\n\n```bash\n# Validate your config file\nflipt validate --config ./flipt.yml\n\n# Or run with debug logging\nflipt --log.level=DEBUG\n```\n\n---\n\n## Bug Fixes\n\nNone in this release.\n\n---\n\n## API Changes\n\n**No breaking API changes** in this release.\n\n- gRPC APIs remain unchanged\n- REST API handlers remain unchanged\n- Protobuf message definitions remain unchanged\n\n---\n\n## Testing & Validation\n\n### Test the New Sampling Feature\n\n```bash\n# Set sampling ratio to 50%\nexport FLIPT_TRACING_SAMPLINGRATIO=0.5\nflipt\n```\n\nCheck your tracing backend to verify that approximately 50% of traces are being collected.\n\n### Test Propagators\n\n```bash\n# Enable multiple propagators for multi-vendor environments\nexport FLIPT_TRACING_PROPAGATORS=\"tracecontext,baggage,b3multi\"\nflipt\n```\n\nVerify that your downstream services receive the trace context headers correctly.\n\n---\n\n## Performance Impact\n\n- **Sampling**: Enabling sampling ratios < 1.0 will reduce CPU and network overhead\n- **Propagators**: Multiple propagators add minimal overhead (microseconds per request)\n- **Resource Attributes**: Minimal impact; attributes are set during initialization, not per request\n\n---\n\n## Documentation References\n\n- [OpenTelemetry Tracing Configuration](./DEVELOPMENT.md#tracing)\n- [Flipt Configuration Schema](./config/flipt.schema.json)\n- [OpenTelemetry Semantic Conventions for Feature Flags](https://opentelemetry.io/docs/specs/semconv/feature-flags/feature-flags-spans/)\n- [OpenTelemetry SDK for Go](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel)\n\n---\n\n## Contributors\n\n- Pablo FLIPT_TRACING_SAMPLINGRATIO=0.1\n```\n\n#### Step 3: Configure Propagators (Optional)\n\nIf you have a multi-vendor tracing setup:\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  propagators:\n    - tracecontext\n    - baggage\n    - b3multi  # Add Zipkin B3 support\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: localhost:4317\n```\n\nOr via environment variable:\n```bash\nexport FLIPT_TRACING_PROPAGATORS=\"tracecontext,baggage,b3multi\"\n```\n\n#### Step 4: Update Jaeger Deployments (If Applicable)\n\nIf you're currently using the Jaeger exporter, migrate to OTLP:\n\n**Old Configuration**:\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: jaeger\n  jaeger:\n    host: jaeger-collector\n    port: 6831\n```\n\n**New Configuration**:\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: jaeger-collector:4317\n```\n\nEnsure your Jaeger collector is configured to receive OTLP:\n```yaml\nreceivers:\n  otlp:\n    protocols:\n      grpc:\n        endpoint: 0.0.0.0:4317\n```\n\n#### Step 5: Validate Configuration\n\n```bash\n# Validate your config file\nflipt validate --config ./flipt.yml\n\n# Or run with debug logging\nflipt --log.level=DEBUG\n```\n\n---\n\n## Bug Fixes\n\nNone in this release.\n\n---\n\n## API Changes\n\n**No breaking API changes** in this release.\n\n- gRPC APIs remain unchanged\n- REST API handlers remain unchanged\n- Protobuf message definitions remain unchanged\n\n---\n\n## Testing & Validation\n\n### Test the New Sampling Feature\n\n```bash\n# Set sampling ratio to 50%\nexport FLIPT_TRACING_SAMPLINGRATIO=0.5\nflipt\n```\n\nCheck your tracing backend to verify that approximately 50% of traces are being collected.\n\n### Test Propagators\n\n```bash\n# Enable multiple propagators for multi-vendor environments\nexport FLIPT_TRACING_PROPAGATORS=\"tracecontext,baggage,b3multi\"\nflipt\n```\n\nVerify that your downstream services receive the trace context headers correctly.\n\n---\n\n## Performance Impact\n\n- **Sampling**: Enabling sampling ratios < 1.0 will reduce CPU and network overhead\n- **Propagators**: Multiple propagators add minimal overhead (microseconds per request)\n- **Resource Attributes**: Minimal impact; attributes are set during initialization, not per request\n\n---\n\n## Documentation References\n\n- [OpenTelemetry Tracing
